### Key Take‑aways
1. **Account health is marginal** – only $0.94 available for new margin; any new trade must respect this limit.  
2. **Open VELVET‑USDT short is profitable** (≈ +$0.44) but **lacks TP/SL**, which violates the safety rule. Immediate action: place appropriate TP and SL for this position.  
3. **Fast pipeline could not execute the intended TAC‑USDT short** because diligence was still running; the system is waiting for confirmation before proceeding.  
4. **Rate‑limit (429) on balance endpoint** forced a disk‑snapshot fallback; the swarm should back‑off and use cached equity data until the API recovers.  
5. **Blocked‑sell list contains the only open position**, so the rule “skip trade if the only candidate is blocked” will prevent any additional short adds this cycle.  

### Recommended Immediate Actions
- **Call `blofin_place_tpsl` (or `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl`)** for `VELVET‑USDT` to add both take‑profit and stop‑loss.  
- **Respect the 429 limit**: pause further balance/position API calls for ~2 minutes, rely on the cached snapshot, and schedule a retry.  
- **Re‑evaluate candidate list** after the diligence step completes; if TAC‑USDT remains viable, attempt the short again (ensuring enough available margin).  
- **Monitor available margin**; with only $0.94 free, any new position must be sized ≤ $0.94 × leverage‑factor (apply `_fit_size_to_available`).
